	build/bootblock/mainboard/emulation/qemu-i440fx/static.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/boot.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/bootblock_romcc.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/cf9_reset.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/cpu_common.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/id.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/memcpy.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/memset.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/mmap_boot.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/timestamp.o build/bootblock/arch/x86/walkcbfs.o build/bootblock/commonlib/cbfs.o build/bootblock/commonlib/iobuf.o build/bootblock/commonlib/lz4_wrapper.o build/bootblock/commonlib/mem_pool.o build/bootblock/commonlib/region.o build/bootblock/console/die.o build/bootblock/console/post.o build/bootblock/console/vsprintf.o build/bootblock/console/vtxprintf.o build/bootblock/cpu/x86/lapic/boot_cpu.o build/bootblock/cpu/x86/mtrr/earlymtrr.o build/bootblock/cpu/x86/pae/pgtbl.o build/bootblock/cpu/x86/tsc/delay_tsc.o build/bootblock/device/device_const.o build/bootblock/device/i2c.o build/bootblock/drivers/pc80/rtc/mc146818rtc.o build/bootblock/drivers/pc80/rtc/mc146818rtc_boot.o build/bootblock/drivers/spi/bitbang.o build/bootblock/drivers/spi/spi-generic.o build/bootblock/drivers/uart/uart8250io.o build/bootblock/drivers/uart/util.o build/bootblock/lib/boot_device.o build/bootblock/lib/bootmode.o build/bootblock/lib/cbfs.o build/bootblock/lib/cbmem_console.o build/bootblock/lib/delay.o build/bootblock/lib/fmap.o build/bootblock/lib/gcc.o build/bootblock/lib/halt.o build/bootblock/lib/hexdump.o build/bootblock/lib/libgcc.o build/bootblock/lib/memchr.o build/bootblock/lib/memcmp.o build/bootblock/lib/prog_loaders.o build/bootblock/lib/prog_ops.o build/bootblock/lib/reset.o build/bootblock/lib/timestamp.o build/bootblock/lib/version.o build/bootblock/southbridge/intel/common/reset.o \
	-T build/bootblock/arch/x86/bootblock.ld
    OBJCOPY    cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf
cp build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.debug build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf.tmp
/root/coreboot/util/crossgcc/xgcc/bin/i386-elf-nm -n build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf.tmp | sort > build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.map
/root/coreboot/util/crossgcc/xgcc/bin/i386-elf-objcopy --strip-debug build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf.tmp
/root/coreboot/util/crossgcc/xgcc/bin/i386-elf-objcopy --add-gnu-debuglink=build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.debug build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf.tmp
mv build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf.tmp build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf
    OBJCOPY    bootblock.raw.elf
/root/coreboot/util/crossgcc/xgcc/bin/i386-elf-objcopy --set-section-flags .bss=load,alloc,data --set-section-flags .data=load,alloc,data build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.elf build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.raw.elf
    OBJCOPY    bootblock.raw.bin
/root/coreboot/util/crossgcc/xgcc/bin/i386-elf-objcopy -O binary build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.raw.elf build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.raw.bin
cp build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.raw.bin build/cbfs/fallback/bootblock.bin
    CC         romstage/mainboard/emulation/qemu-i440fx/static.o

This image contains the following sections that can be manipulated with this tool:

'COREBOOT' (CBFS, size 8388096, offset 512)

It is possible to perform either the write action or the CBFS add/remove actions on every section listed above.
